To answer the 'why eggs and bacon' question: it's all PR! The "father of Public Relations" and nephew of psychoanalyst Sigmund Freud, Edward L. Bernays, worked on a PR campaign for the Beech-Nut Packing Company because, by the 1920s, less manual labor meant lighter breakfasts which meant less bacon sales for Beech-Nut. Bernays managed to round up doctors that chose a heavy breakfast over a light breakfast (on a general survey) and thus, the hearty eggs and bacon all-american breakfast was born.   TLDR; capitalism.

Easy recipe for you to try that has melted vegan cheese! So we do chicken quesadillas (I know you're vegan so sub whatever is appropriate for chicken, or just do "cheese") anyway, so I make gluten-free, dairy-free quesadillas.   Ingredients:  whatever tortillas you prefer vegan cheese taco seasoning (I make my own) Chicken (optional)   Instructions:  Warm tortilla in a skillet on the stove. Flip it to the other side. Layer vegan cheese, sprinkle taco seasoning over all the cheese, add black beans and protein. Add a smidge of cheese just enough to get the tortilla to stick together. Close tortilla, keep on one side 3-5 minutes, flip. Keep on other side 3-5 minutes, done.   I hope someone else who uses vegan cheese finds this useful ğŸ˜… i hated using it until I did this recipe. It literally tastes like queso when melted.   Emma you could stick your breakfast burrito in your new toaster oven thing to see if it melts the cheese!

Fun fact actually! American breakfast has been around for less than a century. You could say it has been a staple since the colonial period. Pigs were easy to domesticate at the time and brining the meat could help preserve it for days before the refrigerator existed! Americans at the time actually only ate porridge and coffee. Bernays ( I don't remember his full name :( but he was the nephew of Sigmund Freud, which is important to remember), was a great salesman and could convince a mass of people to buy products (Again being Freud's nephew and all). He was approached by a company which manufactured and packaged products like pork and bubble gum. They wanted to increase the demand for bacon. So, Freud consulted his agency's doctor to help him know if a heavy breakfast is beneficial for the American public. Later, thousands of doctors researched this and vouched for this idea of a fulfilling breakfast! Plus, the reason why they go so well together is because bacon has nucleotide molecules and eggs have glutamate molecules which together create umami synergy and enhance flavours! Have a good day and grab yourself a plate of bacon and eggs while you're at it!

Answer about eggs and bacon being a traditional breakfast in the U.S: There was a certain guy called Edward Bernays aka "the father of public relations". He was hired by Beech-Nut Packing Company â€“ producers of everything from pork products to the nostalgic Beech-Nut bubble gum. These guys wanted to raise the demand for bacon. What Bernay's did was he decided to make bacon inseparable part of breakfast. Emma, I think your shins hurt when you play drums because if you have a hi-hat and bass drum pedal, both of those pieces require you to work your anterior tibialis (the muscle that runs along your shin bone that's used to bring your foot up from the ground). When I started playing drums that hurt on my leg too, I would recommend gently foam rolling it or even trying some stretching/pilates type exercises to strengthen it. I think it will help with endurance for playing. I love your drum content!!!
